Alone, as if blending into the darkness of the city,
He continued to pursue Revilia.
Vermilion intelligence agency headquarters, conference room bathed in morning sunlight.

Iris' capture of Leon caused an unimaginable stir.

In the past few days,
・A mastermind member of a gang connected behind the scenes
・CEO of the large unscrupulous company Zima Oil
・Leon, an executive of the internationally wanted organization Silver Venom

He is credited with single-handedly accomplishing one after another.
Domestic and international media, intelligence personnel, and even the general public's SNS,
Words like ``Legend of Iris,'' ``Vermilion's White Flash,'' and ``The Strongest Headquarters'' were being thrown around.

A presence that is respected even by Bogdus Javelin――
Even among Vermilion's past top leaders, it was rare to have achieved this much in such a short period of time.

Iris finally returns to the headquarters,
I had my first meeting with Miyushari and Fariel.

When you enter the conference room,
Miyushari waved her hand cheerfully.
Fariel stood there looking a little nervous.

“Director Iris! Finally, I was able to meet you!
This is Miyushari. You're more beautiful than the rumors say."

Miyushari greeted cheerfully,
Fariel next to me suddenly took a step forward with a blushing face.

“Ah, uh… Chief Iris!
I'm... your fan! ! ”

Iris looked out the window at the sunrise,
I whispered quietly.

"Next time, I won't let you escape."
